[30;1m54 | [0m[35m### `--paths-cmd`[0m
[30;1m55 | [0m[35mSome ways to invoke `xargs` will cause multiple `lintrunner` processes to be[0m
[30;1m56 | [0m[35mrun, increasing lint time (especially on huge path sets). As an alternative that[0m
[30;1m57 | [0m[35mgives `lintrunner` control of parallelization, you can use `--paths-cmd`. If[0m
[30;1m58 | [0m[35m`--paths-cmd` is specified `lintrunner` will execute that command and consider[0m
[30;1m59 | [0m[35meach line of its `stdout` to be a file to lint.[0m
[30;1m60 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m120 | [0m[35m## Linter protocol[0m
[30;1m121 | [0m[35mMost linters have their own output format and arguments. In order to impose[0m
[30;1m122 | [0m[35mconsistency on linter invocation and outputs, `lintrunner` implements a protocol[0m
[30;1m123 | [0m[35mthat it expects linters to fulfill. In most cases, a small script (called a[0m
[30;1m124 | [0m[35m*linter adapter*) is required to implement the protocol for a given external[0m
[30;1m125 | [0m[35mlinter. You can see some example adapters in  `examples/` .[0m
[30;1m126 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m53 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m54 | [0m[35m### `--paths-cmd`[0m
[30;1m55 | [0m[35mSome ways to invoke `xargs` will cause multiple `lintrunner` processes to be[0m
[30;1m56 | [0m[35mrun, increasing lint time (especially on huge path sets). As an alternative that[0m
[30;1m57 | [0m[35mgives `lintrunner` control of parallelization, you can use `--paths-cmd`. If[0m
[30;1m58 | [0m[35m`--paths-cmd` is specified `lintrunner` will execute that command and consider[0m
[30;1m59 | [0m[35meach line of its `stdout` to be a file to lint.[0m

[30;1m69 | [0m[35m### `--paths-cmd`[0m
[30;1m70 | [0m[35mSome ways to invoke `xargs` will cause multiple `lintrunner` processes to be[0m
[30;1m71 | [0m[35mrun, increasing lint time (especially on huge path sets). As an alternative that[0m
[30;1m72 | [0m[35mgives `lintrunner` control of parallelization, you can use `--paths-cmd`. If[0m
[30;1m73 | [0m[35m`--paths-cmd` is specified `lintrunner` will execute that command and consider[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35meach line of its `stdout` to be a file to lint.[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m41 | [0m[35mWhen run with no arguments, `lintrunner` will check:[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35m- The files changed in the `HEAD` commit.[0m
[30;1m43 | [0m[35m- The files changed in the user’s working tree.[0m

[30;1m135 | [0m[35m## Linter protocol[0m
[30;1m136 | [0m[35mMost linters have their own output format and arguments. In order to impose[0m
[30;1m137 | [0m[35mconsistency on linter invocation and outputs, `lintrunner` implements a protocol[0m
[30;1m138 | [0m[35mthat it expects linters to fulfill. In most cases, a small script (called a[0m
[30;1m139 | [0m[35m*linter adapter*) is required to implement the protocol for a given external[0m
[30;1m140 | [0m[35mlinter. You can see some example adapters in  `examples/` .[0m
[30;1m141 | [0m[35m[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m285[0m[34m of [0m[33m299[0m[31m ]--[0m

[30;1m68 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m69 | [0m[35m### `--paths-cmd`[0m
[30;1m70 | [0m[35mSome ways to invoke `xargs` will cause multiple `lintrunner` processes to be[0m
[30;1m71 | [0m[35mrun, increasing lint time (especially on huge path sets). As an alternative that[0m
[30;1m72 | [0m[35mgives `lintrunner` control of parallelization, you can use `--paths-cmd`. If[0m
[30;1m73 | [0m[35m`--paths-cmd` is specified `lintrunner` will execute that command and consider[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35meach line of its `stdout` to be a file to lint.[0m
